We come here after a day at the Kern River Preserve. It's a throwback to the old fashion general store with a few extras. The candy selection is out of this world. They have candy that you haven't seen since you were a child. It's fresh and reasonably priced. After that go to the back of the store for a really good deli sandwich! This isn't Subway, this is a huge sandwich (we split one between us). its worth the drive and you can go to the Preserve and picnic there. Check it out while your there and give a donation, they need it and it's a good cause.< /text>

The flowers are in bloom this time of year an make for a great photo opportunity outside. **They have scales here to weigh your vehicle for DMV purposes. <text>Thank you Yelp yet again!

A few days before our move we decided on movers. Since we never used movers in Los Angeles we turned to trusty Yelp to find a moving company.

After some research and phone calls for quotes we decided on NorthStar Movers. With a 4.5 star rating based on 600 some reviews, we knew this company would be a great option. We read through both the good (which is the majority) and bad rated reviews. Not all moves go smoothly, but I can say we just finished our move and it couldn't have gone any better.

Two movers arrived within the appointed time frame. When you schedule your appointment the dispatcher will provide you with a time frame when the movers will arrive. They also gave us a call right before letting us know they were on their way.

The movers who arrived were extremely professional and efficient. Majority of our stuff was already packed so once we let them know what needed to go they worked like a well oiled machine. We had some random items out (since we didn't know what to do with them) and they even offered to help us pack them up.

The movers also came very prepared. They arrived in a 26 foot long truck filled with equipment that made the move more efficient. They had plenty of tape, shrink wrap, and boxes. The movers offered advice as well as I packed up last minute things.

The drive from our old place to our new place was also done in a timely manner. The unloading was just as easy as the loading. I had a desk in my car and they were able to transport that as well. None of our items were damaged in transport.

We couldn't have done this move without NorthStar. When you have employees who are efficient and pleasant to work with, I can't see you going wrong with this moving company. Highly recommended!</text>< Pics>

<review>I live is AZ, and had to move my 91 year old mother from 1 memory care facility to another in Los Angeles. My local mover put me in contact with NorthStar Movers who immediately helped me with a pretty complicated move.  Because of medical reasons, I had to have her things moved within a 4 day window from the time I was notified of the nesseity of the move, coordinate between 3 facilities as to the day and times the move could take place and be able to get to CA to oversee the process on both ends. The result was that there was an open window for alll only on 1 day, between the hours of 12 pm and 3 pm, when the room could be packed, loaded, transported, unloaded, and arranged in the new location, including cleanup. < Text>
As a renter, I have moved a lot. Moving is a pain. Make it less a pain and go with NorthStar.

Here‚Äôs why your pain remedy is NorthStar. During a move, so many things can go wrong‚Äîand for my last move, it seemed everything did. A star guided me to Wendy at NorthStar through those darkest days of moving. NorthStar went so far beyond what anyone could anticipate, I am left in shock. Five gold stars any day of the week.

Miscommunication had taken place, and the building that I was moving into had given away the elevator timeslot. I told NorthStar this, and we rescheduled for the following day to move my items into the new building. NorthStar would hold my items overnight.

Day of the move. I had asked how long it would take to move a 1 bedroom and was told about 4 hours-5 hours. I asked if we could switch my appointment with NorthStar to the afternoon, since I had to work in the morning. When the movers showed up, we only had a few hours to move everything out of a very large 1400-sq-ft 1 bedroom. I had everything packed, except a few unboxed items. We worked at high speed until the building staff said that if we continued, I could receive a fine of over $1,000. NorthStar and I decided to stop. We had moved most of my items out, but we had 8 biggest need-an-elevator  items left: couch, lamp, bookshelf, bar stools, bed, chair, and 2 TVs. While the great Northstar crew were confident that we would figure it out, I felt disheartened and discouraged.

Wasting money is why it was disheartening. Each time the elevator is reserved/used at my old building it is $250, but a whopping $500 at the new building. Having to do a second move meant $750 more in elevator fees alone. Now I‚Äôd also have to pay for a full second day of movers coming and loading, driving, and unloading the truck. I estimated all that would cost at least an additional $1,400 even though it is only 15 miles from downtown Los Angeles to Marina Del Rey. A second day meant an extra $1,400 expenses.

The Wendy Lady
The next day, Wendy called me and asked me about the move and heard about all the issues. She came in eager to solve problems, and that she did. She never tired, and her energy kept me going just when I was ready to give up.

I talked to the staff at the building I was moving from and to, and they said that the soonest I could have the elevator again was Monday. Scheduling problem: Saturday, my current apartment had to be clear because a crew was coming to sand and finish the unit‚Äôs wall-to-wall hardwood floor. Sunday, the cleaning crew would arrive. Monday, I had to give it back to the landlord. With all the items left, how could all that get done?

Wendy took on the challenge and went for it. At first, NorthStar didn‚Äôt have a crew available so I had booked another company, but Wendy was persistent. She said that if Northstar started something, they were going to get the job done. She found another crew, and I was able to get the elevator at my old place.

Wendy and her Northstar crew did get it done. They got the items out of the unit in time for all the work to take place. They offered to waive fees for driving and provide free storage. They really went so far and beyond what even your parents would do it is crazy.  The workers stayed late and drove my stuff to a storage unit that I had rented in Venice to store the items until the other elevator became available. They never stopped working. It was incredible. Furniture piece after furniture piece, they moved.

More companies need to be like NorthStar. Not just get the job done. But take customer service to such an extreme that it is at a level where the customer is wondering what just happened. Who are these people? Companies don‚Äôt do things like this.  But Wendy at NorthStar did.

If you are looking for a moving company whom you can depend on and can hold accountable, NorthStar are your movers.

Thank you, Wendy, for being the star who pointed me in the right direction. Thank you, NorthStar for guiding me get home.<//Text>
